# <a name="microsoft-365-encryption-chains"></a><span data-ttu-id="66e93-103">Microsoft 365 cadenas de cifrado</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="66e93-103">Microsoft 365 encryption chains</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="66e93-104">Microsoft 365 aprovecha una serie de proveedores de certificados diferentes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="66e93-104">Microsoft 365 leverages a number of different certificate providers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="66e93-105">A continuación se describe la lista completa de certificados raíz Microsoft 365 conocidos que los clientes pueden encontrar al obtener acceso a Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="66e93-105">The following describes the complete list of known Microsoft 365 root certificates that customers may encounter when accessing Microsoft 365.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="66e93-106">Para obtener información sobre los certificados que puede que necesite instalar en su propia infraestructura, vea [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="66e93-106">For information on the certificates you may need to install in your own infrastructure, see [Plan for third-party SSL certificates for Microsoft 365](../enterprise/plan-for-third-party-ssl-certificates.md).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="66e93-107">La siguiente información de certificado se aplica a todas las instancias de nube nacionales y mundiales de Microsoft 365.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="66e93-107">The following certificate information applies to all worldwide and national cloud instances of Microsoft 365.</span></span>
